      LEFT JOIN "Users" AS u2 ON o."DeliveredByUserId" = u2."Id"

      LEFT JOIN "Users" AS u2 ON o."DeliveredByUserId" = u2."Id"

      LEFT JOIN "Users" AS u1 ON o."PreparedByUserId" = u1."Id"
      LEFT JOIN "Users" AS u2 ON o."DeliveredByUserId" = u2."Id"
      LEFT JOIN "Payments" AS p ON o."Id" = p."OrderId"
      LEFT JOIN "Events" AS e ON o."EventId" = e."Id"
